; f:\Miranda Translator.NET\Miranda IM\Source\Non-IM Contact 0.5.0.1\dialog.c
[Contacts Display Info]
联系人显示信息
[Link and CList Settings]
链接及联系人列表设置
[Copy Contact]
复制联系人
[String replacing variables....\r\nThe following are all the valid variables that can be used. Refer to the readme for a proper explanation.\r\n\r\n]
字符串替换变量...\r\n以下列所有可以使用的变量. 请参阅帮助获取适当说明. \r\n\r\n
[file(X)\t\t<- specifies the file to read from\r\nMUST be followed by either start() or end() or wholeline()\r\n]
file(X)\t\t<- 指定读入文件\r\n "必须" 跟着 start() 或 end() 或 wholeline()\r\n
[filename(X)\t\t<- copyies the filename of file X.\r\n]
filename(X)\t\t<- 复制文件 X 文件名. \r\n
[start(...)\t\t<-specifies where to start copying from.\r\n]
start(...)\t\t<-指定要开始复制位置. \r\n
[end(...)\t\t<-specifies where to stop copying.\r\n]
end(...)\t\t<-指定要停止复制位置. \r\n
[wholeline(line(...))\t<-specifies a whole line to copy\r\n\r\n]
wholeline(line(...))\t<-指定要复制整列\r\n\r\n
[start() and end() explained\r\n.........................\r\n]
关于 start() 及 end() 说明\r\n.........................\r\n
[MUST start with line() followed by a number or a string inside " marks, OR csv(seperatorX) variable\r\n]
必须以 line() 开始紧跟数字或以 " 标记字符串, 或 csv(分隔符X) 变量\r\n
[The number specifies which character in the line to start/end copying.\r\nThe string specifies a string in the line to start/end copying.\r\n]
该数字指定在句子中要 开始/结束 复制的字符. \r\n字符串则指定在句子中要 开始/结束 复制的文本. \r\n
[csv(seperatorX) explained...\r\nseperator is either "tab" or "space" or any SINGLE character.\r\nX is the Xth seperator to pass before copying, (or to stop before)\r\n\r\n]
csv(分隔符X) 说明...\r\n分隔符可是 "tab" 或 "space" 或任何单一字符. \r\nX 即复制前先跳过 X 个分隔符 (或在停止前)\r\n\r\n
[Lastly the line(...) variable...\r\n]
最后是 line(...) 变量...\r\n
[Inside the brackets must be either a number (to specify the line number), or a string inside " marks (to use the line with that string), or lastline(X).\r\nthe X in lastline is the Xth line above the last line. i.e lastline(1) will use the 2nd last line of the file.\r\n]
在括号内必须是数字 (指定行号), 或在以 " 标记字符串 (使用字符串中句子), 或 lastline(X). \r\nlastline X 是最后一行上方第 X 行. 例如 lastline(1) 将使用文件最后第 2 行. \r\n
[If searching for a line with u may put a + or - X after the closing ) i.e line("some words")+3 to go 3 lines after the line with "some words".\r\n\r\n]
如在句子中进行搜索, 您可在关闭的 ) 后加上 + 或 - X, 即 line("一些字词")+3 前进至含 "一些字词" 句子的后 3 行. \r\n\r\n
[Some Expamples...\r\n\r\n]
一些例子...\r\n\r\n
[filename(0)     <- will display the filename of the 0th file\r\nfile(0)wholeline(line(0))) <- will display the whole first line of the 0th file\r\nfile(0)wholeline(line("hello")-1))) <- the wholeline above the first occurance of "hello" in the file\r\nfile(0)start(line(lastline(1))csv(tab2))end(line(lastline())csv(tab4))) <- starts at the 2nd last line of the file, from the 2nd tab variable, untill the 4th tab variable in the last line (in the 0th file)\r\nfile(0)start(line("hello")+1"zzzz")end(line(6)17)) <- starts from the first occurance of zzzz in the line after the first occurance of hello, untill the 17th character in the 6th line (starting from line 0) of the 0th file.\r\n]
filename(0)     <- 将显示第 0 个文件的文件名称\r\nfile(0)wholeline(line(0))) <- 将显示第 0 个文件第一行的整行\r\nfile(0)wholeline(line("您好")-1))) <- wholeline 应用于文件内第一个出现 "您好" 的句子\r\nfile(0)start(line(lastline(1))csv(tab2))end(line(lastline())csv(tab4))) <- 开始于文件的最后第 2 行, 由第 2 个分栏变量开始, 直至最后一行的第 4 个分栏变量 (在第 0 个文件)\r\nfile(0)start(line("hello")+1"zzzz")end(line(6)17)) <- 由第 0 个文件中第一个出现您好的句子后面出现第一个 zzzz 的行开始, 直至第 6 行的第 17 个字符 (由第 0 行开始). \r\n

[&New phrase/pattern:]

[(You can use normal words or Regular Expressions)]
(您可使用标准字词或正则表达式)
[Quick Quide to Regular Expressions:]
正则表达式快速导览: 
[Alternatives:]
备选方案: 
[gilbert|sullivan finds "gilbert" or "sullivan"]
gilbert|sullivan 查找 "gilbert" 或 "sullivan"
[Subpatterns:]
子样式: 
[cat(aract|erpillar) finds "cataract" or "caterpillar"]
cat(aract|erpillar) 查找 "cataract" 或 "caterpillar"
[Repetitions:]
重复: 
[z{2,4} matches "zz", "zzz" or "zzzz"\r\n* is equivalent to {0,}\r\n+ is equivalent to {1,}\r\n? is equivalent to {0,1}]
z{2,4} 符合 "zz", "zzz" 或 "zzzz"\r\n* 等同于 {0,}\r\n+ 等同于 {1,}\r\n? 等同于 {0,1}
[Generic Types:]
一般类型: 
[\\d represents any decimal digit\r\n\\D represents any character that is not a decimal digit]
\\d 代表任何十进制数字\r\n\\D 代表任何非十进制数字字符
[Assertions:]
断言: 
[(?<!foo)bar finds an occurrence of "bar" that is not preceded by "foo"\r\n(?<= for positive lookahead assertions\r\n(?<! for negative lookahead assertions\r\n(?= for positive lookbehind assertions\r\n(?! for negative lookbehind assertions]
(?<!foo)bar 查找未使用 "foo" 开头的 "bar"\r\n(?<= 正值前向界定符\r\n?<! 负值前向界定符\r\n(?= 正值后向界定符\r\n(?! 负值后向界定符
[Back References:]
反向参照: 
[(sens|respons)e and \\1ibility matches "sense and sensibility" and "response and responsibility", but not "sense and responsibility"]
(sens|respons)e and \\1ibility 符合 "sense and sensibility" 及 "response and responsibility", 但不符合 "sense and responsibility"

所有语法元素可合并或嵌套使用子模式

[Here's a next sequence to play:]
这里是游戏下一轮:
[1. You have to make the handshake. For this you have to press "New game" button. This one sends a request to your opponent. When you got his answer the game will start.\n2. The game will start with ship arrangement. You must move all available ships from a right side into a left. Use a left-click to take/drop a ship. A right mouse button is toggle a direction of a ship.\n3. When you will finish your arrangement you have to press the "Ready!" button. If your opponent isn't ready the appropriate message will shown in the status bar.\n4. Current state of the game is reflected in the status bar.\nGood luck and have fun!]
1. 您必须握手. 为此您必须按下 "新游戏" 按钮. 这将给您的对手发送一个邀请. 当您得到他的答复时游戏将开始.\n2. 游戏开始先要布置舰船. 您必须从右侧将所有可用舰船移至左侧. 使用左键拿起/放下舰船. 右键切换舰船方向.\n3. 当您完成布置时需按下 "准备!" 按钮. 如您的对手尚未准备好状态栏将显示相关信息.\n4. 当前游戏状态也将显示于状态栏中.\n祝您好运, 玩得高兴!

[StopSpam mod]
StopSpam 模块
[No more spam! Robots can't go! Only human beings invited!\r\n\r\nThis plugin works pretty simple:\r\nWhile messages from users on your contact list go as there is no any anti-spam software, messages from unknown users are not delivered to you. But also they are not ignored, this plugin replies with a simple question, and if user gives the right answer plugin adds him to your contact list so that he can contact you.]
无垃圾! 机器人! 仅邀请人类!\r\n\r\n此插件非常简单:\r\n您的联系人列表用户消息则放行, 不使用任何反垃圾软件, 未知联系人消息则阻拦. 但并非忽略, 此插件回复一个简单问题, 如用户提供了正确答案, 插件则将其加至您的联系人列表以便沟通.
[Autoreply to auth. requests]
自动答复 认证 请求

[Remove Temporary Contacts]

[Ignore Authorization requests with URL]
忽略包含链接的授权请示
[Avaible accounts:]
可用帐号:
[It remains to attempt:]
依然尝试:
[The last attempt!]
最后尝试!
[Spammers made me to install small anti-spam system you are now speaking with.Please reply "nospam" without quotes and spaces if you want to contact me.]
现在与您聊天的是为应付垃圾邮件寄件者而安装的小型反垃圾邮件系统.如果您想与我聊天,请回复 "nospam" 无引号和空格.
[Use regex for answers checking]
使用正则表达式检查答案
[Log Spammers to system history]
